Headnote

Summary: This work is a bibliographic repertoire of the Spanish short theater from 2000 to 2010, in which it has been intended authors. Some playwrights have been taken into account that, although born abroad, have acquired Spanish nationality, have been based in Spain or are closely linked to the dramaturgy of our country. For its management, an ordination by surnames of each author has been carried out and within these chronological of their works.

Abstract: This Paper is a Repertory of the Short Spanish Theater Literature from 2000 to 2010, Which has Sought to discuss the Maximun Number of Short Plays Published in Spain in Spanish: More than Thirteen Hundrend, from Six Sinkred Authors,. It has been taken into accouunt sum authors who, though born abroad, Have Acquire Spanish Nationality, have settled in Spain, or are closely connected with the drama of our country. For an Easy Handling has been overd by last of Each Author and Within these, By Works Chronology.

Keywords: Bibliographic. Spanish Short Theater. New Millennium (2000- 2010). Spanish language. Authors born or Spanish nationality.

Key Words: Bibliography. Short Spanish Theater. The New Millenium (2000- 2010). Spanish Language. Spanish Authors.

I. Notes on this bibliography

The objective of this work is to collect the conclusions derived from the bibliographic compilation of the Spanish short theater since the beginning of the 21st century to the present day1, which I have carried out, in which it has been intended to include the maximum number of brief plays published In Spain, in Castilian language. Works of some playwrights have been taken into account that, although born abroad, have acquired Spanish nationality, have been based in Spain or are closely linked to the dramaturgy of our country. The amount of short pieces published in the new millennium is overwhelming: more than a thousand three hundred, belonging to six hundred authors (referred, of course, to what I collect).

The concept of brief theater covers from the shortest piece, the micropiere, minimum piece, dramatic flea or what Jesús Campos has called as a "transgenic", that of the very brief, of just a few lines, whose dramatic situation is resolved in the Short space of a minute, until the largest that, depending on the publication format, does not usually exceed forty pages2 and on stage do not exceed ninety minutes. The urgent character of the shortest pieces extends even to the time they have been written, just a few days or hours3. The first commandment that Gustavo Montes dictates in his trilogy of theater Hurgente (2005: 17) is the intensity of his works and a duration around half an hour in a single stage. TAT emphasis is product of a monographic monographic seized in our contemporaryity and a half of support from the collective carpet of autore destinents distinct for social political causes (campic García, 2006: 9). It is the case of the ATT the sea (2003), solidarity with Galicia, cuyos texts that are mainly selected for funds for help to go to the disaster of ecological ecry of the prefix. Other Initiatives of the Association of Theater Awards Found the Teatro against War (2003), where it was fifty and two texts with the Iraq war, and eleven voces against the 11-M, writtenhorror of the terrorist blow and in memory of the victims. In anthology Exiles: 18 plays of Argentine, Spanish and Mexican authors (2003), also their authors share a historical experience when dealing with the issue of exile in its broadest sense, not only from which it occurs for political reasons or political reasons economic, but also that it is a consequence of oneself. The same line is found in the key: a project from Madrid South (June, 1999), of the year 2005, whose texts collect reflections on Spanish exile. The eighty -nine scream monologues: I have AIDS!, Published in 2006, at the initiative of the Association of Theater Authors, they are indicative of the proximity of the authors with the most hot social issues of our news. Also the confession (2001) joins the set of anthologies that offer a panoramic view of the most intimate concerns of today's human beings, through the way of recognizing and relief that confession offers.

Some anthologies have been promoted by workshops and dramatic art schools, which include texts of younger playwrights, in search of new scenic palapitos. It should be noted in this sense the short pieces of the students of the Royal Superior School of Dramatic Art (Resad), the most important dramatic art institution in Spain today. The anthologies of brief pieces of the resad have been published since the beginning of Millennium to the present day. Thus, for an example of the result of one of the promotions, the theater volume: short pieces 2001-2002 (2002) collects the most representative pieces of the writing practices of the subject "Theory and practice of dramatic writing II", Taught by Daniel Sarasola, in which he invited to investigate in this case on a subject such as the Mold of the Aristophalanic comedy. They saw their writings Belén Franco Dada, Jesús Laiz and Zara Paniagua.

To a lesser extent, other workshops have also been and continue to be the focus of the new dramaturgies. Thus, the Umheimliche-Lo sinister (2002) anthology was carried out by the dramatic writing workshop during the months of March to June 2001, in the Athenaeum of Madrid, promoted by the Astillero Theater Association, which sought a reflection from the Scene about Sigmud Freud's text "The sinister." The workshop was coordinated by Guillermo Heras and Juan Mayorga, Raúl Hernández Garrido, José Ramón Fernández, Luis Miguel González Cruz and Guillermo Heras participated as professors. In addition, eleven short pieces are written by students. Also in order to complete the formation of the actor with the incorporation of dramatic writing in his educational project, something previously non -existent, arises from the Dramatic Writing Workshop of the BAI -Bizkaiko Antzerki Ikastegia- the anthology more than words (2002), in which participated by young actors and actresses involved to playwrights with twelve pieces. Four years later, the same workshop published Polaroids, with nineteen pieces, small polaroids, of the students of the first four-month period of the 2005-2006 academic year, taught by Josu Montero.

Marriages anthology, from 2006, emerged from the dramatic writing laboratory that Guillermo Heras made a reality within the sample of Author Author. Guillermo HeraS intended to configure it as a continuous space for reflection, as a permanent dramaturgy center, not only for the sample. The result is a set of very different writings around the proposal of the different perspectives and dissident concepts today. Again, in order to enhance new theatrical writing routes, the XVI Spanish Theater Sample of Contemporary Authors, after three -year labor, published the anthology around random (2008).

We cannot fail to mention a series of brief theater anthologies, which because this is a very suitable format, they intend to offer a current short theater impulse, through the incorporation of the greatest number of representative authors and that have been published in 2006, multiplying the number of pieces of this year in particular. As Ramón Espejo Romero (2006: 5) points out in spite Starting from the rebirth of the short theater in the 1980s and, above all, in the 1990s, dramatic writing has been silenced on many occasions. An answer to this lack is the volume published by the Documentation Center for the Performing Arts of Andalusia, Brief Andalusian Theater (2006), which includes twelve short pieces, and especially 60 works in 1 minute of 60 Andalusian dramatic authors, where authors of the three generations and of the most varied artistic and dramaturgical experiences collaborate with a minute of approximately one minute to celebrate World Theater Day of 2006 and with the possibility that they were represented in a single session by the students of the students of the Higher School of Dramatic Arts of Seville.

The texts of these anthologies are works that have their own value and meaning, but they also form a singular artistic work: «They are autonomous works, with their characteristics and points of view, but at the same time each of them serves as a counterpoint, of contrast , of reaffirmation and complement of the other pieces to form an altarpiece, perhaps not polychrome, of the difference ”(López Dávila, 2004: 5).

It is noteworthy the work of Jesús Campos García, as President of the Association of Theater Authors (AAT) 6, through whom the Spanish short theater has received an unusual impulse and dissemination, thanks to the publication of dramatic texts and organization of numerous cycles of dramatized readings. Alberto Milares, as secretary of the AAT, began the publication of four volumes with short monologues, sometimes more than forty, who saw the light under the marathon title of monologues since 2002 and who have subsequently been published until 2008. The 2009 marathon has not seen the printed form, although you can access the dramatized reading of its texts on YouTube, as well as that of 2010, whose dramatized reading took place, organized by the Association of Theater Authors, in the house on from Madrid, on June 4, 2010. Other of the co-teaching demonstrations launched by the ATT have been the rapid writing awards «Express Theater», which have been edited since 2001 with the title of Express Theater 2000 until 2007.

At the rise of brief theater he has contributedIn an outstanding way Eduardo Quiles through the direction of Art Theatrical magazine, specialized in Brief Theater, directed by the playwright until 2008. José Moreno Arenas also directs the theatrical section of the prestigious literary magazine Alhucema, in whose numbers Publishing, since its creation, pieces of the best brief and minimum theater of the most diverse authors of the current scenic panorama. They also contain among their pages a good number of short pieces the first act, the theater research magazine dimensions, published by the editorial foundations under the direction of Ricardo Doménech, who founded it in 1998, and later, since 2008, of the playwright Pedro Víllora, the Galician theater magazine, whose works are often translated into Spanish, the magazine of theory and practice of Hispanic theater gestures, etc. Other periodic publications that include short theater are theater (from the Association of Stage Directors of Spain), the SIGNA magazine (edited by the Literary, Theater Semiotics Research Center and New Technologies of the UNED; under the direction of José Romera Castillo, in printed and electronic format: http: cervantesvirtual. Com/hemeroteca/sign), the premiere magazine, notebooks of contemporary Spanish theater, modern theater (of the delegation of culture of the City of Chiclana de la Frontera), the truce (the truce (the truce ( from Alcalá la Real, Jaén), Abracadabra. Literary Magazine (De Cádiz), SIE7E Notebook (directed by Leandro Herrero, the City of Coslada and Department of Culture of Madrid), in figurative sense (since November 11, 2007) 7, among others.

No less incentives offer for the writing of the Brief Theater the Caja España Brief Theater Awards, Miguel Romeo Esteo, "Doña Mencía de Salcedo", Cajamadrid de Theater Express, "Andalusian" Prize for Brief Theater (since 2000) or the "Rafael Guerrero Guerrero Guerrero »Minimum theater, among others.

To the claim of the Short Theater of Women and for Women in the New Millennium, the three cycles of the Marias Guerreras have collaborated in the house of America in the years 2004, 2005 and 2006, and the women's anthologies on women at the dawn of the century XXI: Brief Theater, by P. W. O'Connor (2006) and women for women: Brief Theater (2009).

The main thematic concern of the short pieces today is not only political, but also social. As indicated by Berta Muñoz Cáliz, (2006: 21), there is "a certain resurgence of a brief theater with a vocation to intervene in social life", since the late 90s, whose beginnings, on the other hand, manifest, as they manifest, as María Jesús Orozco Vera points out, "from the 80s, reaching a greater boom in the newly initiated 21st century" (2006b: 30-31) 8. Virtues Serrano highlights how «the events that have come to fill the historical reality of the early 21st century have soon been noticed in the issues of the latest works appeared, both in extensive dramatic literature and in the lesser format pieces [ ...]. The unusual violence that has been downloaded in the known world, expressed in wars, attacks, reprisals, killings and destruction has soon echoed in the current dramaturgy, which has been filled with perplexities, anguish, discouragement and allegations, against terrorism, against the injustice of the strongest,against imperialism and against genocides. The theater continues to fulfill in this century the testimonial mission that had been entrusted from the past: being a mirror of life and customs and reflection of the conflicts of the beings of their surroundings ”(Serrano, 2004: 24).

For his part, Fernando Doménech coincides with this idea in theater: RESAD RESAD COURSE 1998-2002, where “nine plays appear with a vocation to tell the world in which we live, to unravel the keys to this society more opaque and without However, more and more simple mechanisms, where oppression, poverty, moral and material misery disguise themselves with new perceptions that fail to hide the enormity of injustice and restlessness ”(Doménech, 2003: 7). A historical reality that Pozas Street relates to the reality that the media manifest and that in turn reflects the Hurgost theater. The stories that make up Off Familia's, by Gustavo Montes (2005: 10-11), come from three different journalistic news, unified thematically by the weight that the family concept has in the behavior of the characters.

War is one of the most discussed themes, not only on the occasion of Iraq, but also in relation to any war or all wars, as expresses the subtitle of Margarita Reiz's piece, «everything will go well. Actions, documents, words and images around war, any war, all wars ... »(2005: 107). An issue related to this is the denunciation of the power that the fort exercises over the weak. José Luis Miranda, being part of the Jury of the IV Contest of theatrical Texts «Miguel Romeo Esteo» for young Andalusian authors, was surprised that in most of the twenty -five texts presented, there was a theme that revolved around «a certain concern about record the abuse of power - social, political, economic - on the dispossessed ”(Miranda, 2001: 3).

According to Sanchis Sinisterra, "a considerable sector of the most recent generation of authors, endowed with a high level of creativity, seems dedicated to discussing issues and circumstances circumscribed to the next, private, intimidist" (2001: 11). This was said on the occasion of the texts made in the dramatic writing workshop, directed by him, where photographs with a shiver Dramatic cell that will project its suggestive force in the sensitivity and awareness of a dramaturgical collective. As Ecos and Silences point out in the same anthology, the directors Jesús Crio and Roberto Cerdá, it was intended that the playwrights converge in a common point: «approaching those people to imagine what they feel and how they live, how they suffer and what dream [.. .] With the desire to ask ourselves about the state of the world we are creating and that quickly devours us without realizing it. Injustice lives at ease and is no longer enough to feel outrage ”(2001: 9).

Finally, the problematic relations between human beings is another of the most frequented issues, whether as a couple, friendship or family.
